    var mktautoreftime = "100000";
    $(document).ready(function () {
        $("#searchhp").validationEngine();
        createDropDown();
        $(".dropdown dt a").click(function () {
            $(".dropdown dd ul").toggle();
        });
        $(document).bind('click', function (e) {
            var $clicked = $(e.target);
            if (!$clicked.parents().hasClass("dropdown"))
                $(".dropdown dd ul").hide();
        });
        $(".dropdown dd ul li a").click(function () {
            var text = $(this).html();
            $(".dropdown dt a").html(text);
            $(".dropdown dd ul").hide();
            //$("#result").html("Selected value is: " + getSelectedValue("target"));
            var source = $("#searchcategory");
            source.val($(this).find("span.value").html());
        });
        $(".searchdropdown li a").click(function () {
            var a = $(this).attr('data-input');
            if ($(this).attr('value') == 'news') {
                $("#" + a).autocomplete({
                    disabled: true
                });
            }
            else {
                $("#" + a).autocomplete({
                    disabled: false
                });
            }
        });
        $('.searchsubmit').click(function () {
            var keyword2 = $('#' + $(this).attr('data-input')).val();
            var keyword2 = keyword2.replace(/[`~!@#$%^&*()_|+\-=?;:'",.<>\{\}\[\]\\\/]/gi, '+');
            var keyword2 = keyword2.replace(/[^A-Z0-9]/ig, "_");
            var keyword2 = keyword2.replace(/[^A-Z0-9]+/ig, "+");
            var keyword3 = $('#' + $(this).attr('data-keyword')).val();
            if (keyword2 != "") {
                if (keyword3 == 'News') {
                    window.location.href = "/search/news/" + keyword2;
                    //window.location.href = "/search/news/" + encodeURIComponent(keyword2);
                    return false;
                } else {
                    window.location.href = "/search/quotes/" + keyword2;
                    return false;
                }
            }
            else
            {
                alert('Please provide your search input !!');
                return false;
            }
        });

        $('.yt-videos').click(function () {
            var ytVideoLink = $(this).attr('data-url');
            $("#tvVideo").attr("src", ytVideoLink);
        });

		$('.utubevideo1').click(function(){
			var videoId = $(this).attr('data-id');
			$("#tvVideo").attr("src", videoId);
        });
		
		$('#myModal').click(function () {
            $("#tvVideo").attr("src", '');
        });
    });

     function getSelectedValue(el) {
     var a = $("#"+el).val();
     a = a.toLowerCase();
     a = a.replace(' ','');
     return a;

    function getSelectedValue() {

        var a = $("#searchcategory").val();
        a = a.toLowerCase();
        a = a.replace(' ', '');
        return a;
    }

    function getSelectedValueSticky() {

        var a = $("#searchcategorySticky").val();
        a = a.toLowerCase();
        a = a.replace(' ', '');
        return a;
    }

    function getSelectedValueMobile() {

        var a = $("#searchcategoryMobile").val();
        a = a.toLowerCase();
        a = a.replace(' ', '');
        return a;
    }

    function createDropDown() {
        var source = $("#searchcategory");
        var selected = source.find("option[selected]");
        var options = $("option", source);
        $("#searchcategorydl").append('<dl id="target" class="dropdown"></dl>')
        $("#target").append('<dt><a href="javascript:void(0);">' + selected.text() +
                '<span class="value">' + selected.val() +
                '</span></a></dt>')
        $("#target").append('<dd><ul></ul></dd>')
        options.each(function () {
            $("#target dd ul").append('<li><a href="javascript:void(0);">' +
                    $(this).text() + '<span class="value">' +
                    $(this).val() + '</span></a></li>');
        });
    }

    $(function () {
        var pgurl = window.location.href;
        var indexval = pgurl.indexOf("/", 10);
        var realhref = pgurl.substr(indexval, (pgurl.length) + 1);
        $(".navbar-nav >li> a").each(function () {
            if ($(this).attr("href") == realhref || $(this).attr("href") == '') {
                $(".navbar-nav >li> a").removeClass('active');
                $(this).addClass("active");
            }
        })
        $(".navbar-nav >li>ul.mega-dropdown-menu li a").each(function () {
            if ($(this).attr("href") == realhref || $(this).attr("href") == '') {
                $(".navbar-nav >li> a").removeClass('active');
                $(this).addClass("active");
                $(this).parents('.mega-dropdown').find('.dropdown-toggle').addClass("active");
            }
        })
    });

	getchartData1 = JSON.parse(getchartData);

	AmCharts.ready( function() {
	  generateChartData();
	  createStockChart();
	} );

	var chart;
	var chartData = [];
	var newPanel;
	var stockPanel;

	function generateChartData() {
	   chartData = getchartData1;
	}

	function createStockChart() {
	  chart = new AmCharts.AmStockChart();
	  chart.balloon.horizontalPadding = 13;

	  // DATASET //////////////////////////////////////////
	  var dataSet = new AmCharts.DataSet();
	  
	  dataSet.fieldMappings = [ {
		fromField: "open",
		toField: "open"
	  }, {
		fromField: "close",
		toField: "close"
	  }, {
		fromField: "high",
		toField: "high"
	  }, {
		fromField: "low",
		toField: "low"
	  }, {
		fromField: "volume",
		toField: "volume"
	  }, {
		fromField: "value",
		toField: "value"
	  } ];
	  dataSet.color = "#d9d9d9";
	  dataSet.dataProvider = chartData;
	  dataSet.categoryField = "date";
	  /*dataSet.dataDateFormat = "MM-DD-YYYY JJ:NN:SS";*/
	  dataSet.borderAlpha = "1";

	  chart.dataSets = [ dataSet ];

	  // PANELS ///////////////////////////////////////////                                                  
	  stockPanel = new AmCharts.StockPanel();
	  stockPanel.title = "Value";

	  // graph of first stock panel
	  var graph = new AmCharts.StockGraph();
	  graph.type = "line";
	  graph.openField = "open";
	  graph.closeField = "close";
	  graph.highField = "high";
	  graph.lowField = "low";
	  graph.valueField = "close";
	  graph.lineColor = "#008fc5";
	  /*graph.fillColors = "#b2e7fa";*/
	  graph.fillColors = ["#b2e7fa","#fff"];
	  graph.negativeLineColor = "#f16e2d";
	  graph.negativeFillColors = "#f7b796";
	  graph.fillAlphas = 1;
	  graph.balloonText = "Open:<b>[[open]]</b><br>Close:<b>[[close]]</b><br>Low:<b>[[low]]</b><br>High:<b>[[high]]</b>";
	  graph.useDataSetColors = false;
	  stockPanel.addStockGraph( graph );
	  chart.panels = [ stockPanel ];

	  // OTHER SETTINGS ////////////////////////////////////
	  var sbsettings = new AmCharts.ChartScrollbarSettings();
	  sbsettings.graph = graph;
	  sbsettings.graphType = "line";
	  sbsettings.usePeriod = "WW";
	  chart.chartScrollbarSettings = sbsettings;

	  // Enable pan events
	  var panelsSettings = new AmCharts.PanelsSettings();
	  panelsSettings.panEventsEnabled = true;
	  chart.panelsSettings = panelsSettings;

	  // CURSOR
	  var cursorSettings = new AmCharts.ChartCursorSettings();
	  cursorSettings.valueBalloonsEnabled = true;
	  cursorSettings.valueLineBalloonEnabled = true;
	  cursorSettings.valueLineEnabled = true;
	  chart.chartCursorSettings = cursorSettings;

	  // PERIOD SELECTOR ///////////////////////////////////
	  var periodSelector = new AmCharts.PeriodSelector();
	  periodSelector.position = "bottom";
	  periodSelector.inputFieldsEnabled = false;
	  periodSelector.periods = [ {
		period: "DD",
		count: 7,
		label: "7d"
	  }, {
		period: "MM",
		count: 1,
		label: "1m"
	  }, {
		period: "MM",
		count: 3,
		label: "3m"
	  }, {
		period: "MM",
		count: 6,
		label: "6m"
	  }, {
		period: "YYYY",
		count: 1,
		label: "1y"
	  }, {
		period: "YYYY",
		count: 2,
		label: "2y"
	  }, {
		period: "YYYY",
		count: 3,
		label: "3y"
	  }, {
		period: "YTD",
		label: "YTD"
	  }, {
		period: "MAX",
		selected: true,
		label: "MAX"
	  } ];
	  chart.periodSelector = periodSelector;
	  
	  chart["export"] = {
		enabled: true
	  };
	  
	  chart.write( 'chartdiv' );
	}

	function addPanel() {
	  newPanel = new AmCharts.StockPanel();
	  newPanel.allowTurningOff = false;
	  newPanel.title = "Volume";
	  newPanel.showCategoryAxis = false;
	  newPanel.valueAxes.dashLength = 5;
		
	  var graph = new AmCharts.StockGraph();
	  graph.valueField = "volume";
	  graph.type = "column";
	  graph.fillAlphas = 1;
	  newPanel.addStockGraph( graph );

	  var legend = new AmCharts.StockLegend();
	  legend.markerType = "none";
	  legend.markerSize = 0;
	  newPanel.stockLegend = legend;

	  chart.addPanelAt( newPanel, 1 );
	  chart.validateNow();
	  /*document.getElementById( "addPanelButton" ).disabled = true;
	  document.getElementById( "removePanelButton" ).disabled = false;*/
	}

	function removePanel() {
	  chart.removePanel( newPanel );
	  chart.validateNow();

	  document.getElementById( "AddRemoveVolume" ).checked = false;
	  /*document.getElementById( "addPanelButton" ).disabled = false;
	  document.getElementById( "removePanelButton" ).disabled = true;*/
	}

	function changeType(type) {
	  chart.panels[0].stockGraphs[0].type = type;
	  chart.validateNow();
	}

$(document).ready(function(){
	$("#email_form").validationEngine();
	reloadCaptcha();
	
	$('.rsave').click(function(){
		var aid = '116122000288';
		$.ajax({
			type : 'POST',
			url : '/article/save-user-article/',
			data : { aid:aid},
			success : function(data){
				if(data == 1){
				$('#savediv').hide();
				$('#savemsg').fadeIn().delay(3000).fadeOut();
				}else{
					$('#savediv').hide();
					$('#errormsg').show();
				}
			}
		});
	});
});

$('#email_popup').on('click', function(){
		$.ajax({
			type: 'POST',
			url: "/article/email",
			data:{ 
				'articleSeoStr' : $("#articleSeoStr").val(),
				'categorySeoStr' : $("#categorySeoStr").val(), 
				'name' : $("#name").val(), 
				'email' : $("#mail").val(),
				'friendEmail' : $("#friendEmail").val(), 
				'msg' : $("#msg").val(),
				'rcmtno' : $("#rcmtno").val(),
				'chitos_user':$("#chitos_user").val()
			},
			
			success: function(res){ 
								// $('.result_popup').fadeOut(1000);
								$('.result_popup').html( res ).show();
								// setTimeout(function(){
									// $("#emailModal").hide();
								// }, 3000);
			}
		});
});

function shownewsgraph_maindata(tabid){
	$('#mkt_tab_content_'+tabid).parents('.inner').find('.mkt_tab_content').hide();
	$('#showmkt_maintab_'+tabid).parents('.inner').find('.news_chart a').removeClass('active');
	$('#showmkt_maintab_'+tabid).addClass('active');
	$('#mkt_tab_content_'+tabid).fadeToggle();
}

function reloadCaptcha(){           
	$("#img_chitos").removeAttr("src");
	var randNo = Math.floor((Math.random() * 48) + 1);
	$("#img_chitos").attr("src", "/captcha/" + randNo);
	$("#rcmtno").val(randNo);
}

reloadCaptcha();

    function DropDown(el) {
        this.dd = el;
        this.initEvents();
    }
    DropDown.prototype = {
        initEvents: function () {
            var obj = this;

            obj.dd.on('click', function (event) {
                $(this).addClass('active');
                event.stopPropagation();
            });
        }
    }
    $(function () {
        var dd = new DropDown($('#dd'));
        $('.wrapper-dropdown-5').mouseleave(function () {
            // all dropdowns
            $('.wrapper-dropdown-5').removeClass('active');
        });
    });

    function mycarousel_initCallback(carousel) {
        carousel.clip.hover(function () {
            carousel.stopAuto();
        }, function () {
            carousel.startAuto();
        });
    }

                $('.iifl_acc_div').slideUp();

        $('#mkt_tabs_cont_' + tabid).fadeToggle();
    }

    }

        }
    }

    var mktautoreftime = "100000";
    $(document).ready(function () {
        $("#searchhp").validationEngine();
        createDropDown();
        $(".dropdown dt a").click(function () {
            $(".dropdown dd ul").toggle();
        });
        $(document).bind('click', function (e) {
            var $clicked = $(e.target);
            if (!$clicked.parents().hasClass("dropdown"))
                $(".dropdown dd ul").hide();
        });
        $(".dropdown dd ul li a").click(function () {
            var text = $(this).html();
            $(".dropdown dt a").html(text);
            $(".dropdown dd ul").hide();
            //$("#result").html("Selected value is: " + getSelectedValue("target"));
            var source = $("#searchcategory");
            source.val($(this).find("span.value").html());
        });
        $(".searchdropdown li a").click(function () {
            var a = $(this).attr('data-input');
            if ($(this).attr('value') == 'news') {
                $("#" + a).autocomplete({
                    disabled: true
                });
            }
            else {
                $("#" + a).autocomplete({
                    disabled: false
                });
            }
        });
        $('.searchsubmit').click(function () {
            var keyword2 = $('#' + $(this).attr('data-input')).val();
            var keyword2 = keyword2.replace(/[`~!@#$%^&*()_|+\-=?;:'",.<>\{\}\[\]\\\/]/gi, '+');
            var keyword2 = keyword2.replace(/[^A-Z0-9]/ig, "_");
            var keyword2 = keyword2.replace(/[^A-Z0-9]+/ig, "+");
            var keyword3 = $('#' + $(this).attr('data-keyword')).val();
            if (keyword2 != "") {
                if (keyword3 == 'News') {
                    window.location.href = "/search/news/" + keyword2;
                    //window.location.href = "/search/news/" + encodeURIComponent(keyword2);
                    return false;
                } else {
                    window.location.href = "/search/quotes/" + keyword2;
                    return false;
                }
            }
            else
            {
                alert('Please provide your search input !!');
                return false;
            }
        });

        $('.yt-videos').click(function () {
            var ytVideoLink = $(this).attr('data-url');
            $("#tvVideo").attr("src", ytVideoLink);
        });

		$('.utubevideo1').click(function(){
			var videoId = $(this).attr('data-id');
			$("#tvVideo").attr("src", videoId);
        });
		
		$('#myModal').click(function () {
            $("#tvVideo").attr("src", '');
        });
    });

    function getSelectedValue() {

        var a = $("#searchcategory").val();
        a = a.toLowerCase();
        a = a.replace(' ', '');
        return a;
    }

    function getSelectedValueSticky() {

        var a = $("#searchcategorySticky").val();
        a = a.toLowerCase();
        a = a.replace(' ', '');
        return a;
    }

    function getSelectedValueMobile() {

        var a = $("#searchcategoryMobile").val();
        a = a.toLowerCase();
        a = a.replace(' ', '');
        return a;
    }

    function createDropDown() {
        var source = $("#searchcategory");
        var selected = source.find("option[selected]");
        var options = $("option", source);
        $("#searchcategorydl").append('<dl id="target" class="dropdown"></dl>')
        $("#target").append('<dt><a href="javascript:void(0);">' + selected.text() +
                '<span class="value">' + selected.val() +
                '</span></a></dt>')
        $("#target").append('<dd><ul></ul></dd>')
        options.each(function () {
            $("#target dd ul").append('<li><a href="javascript:void(0);">' +
                    $(this).text() + '<span class="value">' +
                    $(this).val() + '</span></a></li>');
        });
    }

    $(function () {
        var pgurl = window.location.href;
        var indexval = pgurl.indexOf("/", 10);
        var realhref = pgurl.substr(indexval, (pgurl.length) + 1);
        $(".navbar-nav >li> a").each(function () {
            if ($(this).attr("href") == realhref || $(this).attr("href") == '') {
                $(".navbar-nav >li> a").removeClass('active');
                $(this).addClass("active");
            }
        })
        $(".navbar-nav >li>ul.mega-dropdown-menu li a").each(function () {
            if ($(this).attr("href") == realhref || $(this).attr("href") == '') {
                $(".navbar-nav >li> a").removeClass('active');
                $(this).addClass("active");
                $(this).parents('.mega-dropdown').find('.dropdown-toggle').addClass("active");
            }
        })
    });

	AmCharts.ready( function() {
	  generateChartData();
	  createStockChart();
	} );

	var chart;
	var chartData = [];
	var newPanel;
	var stockPanel;

	function generateChartData() {
	   chartData = getchartData1;
	}

	function createStockChart() {
	  chart = new AmCharts.AmStockChart();
	  chart.balloon.horizontalPadding = 13;

	  // DATASET //////////////////////////////////////////
	  var dataSet = new AmCharts.DataSet();
	  
	  dataSet.fieldMappings = [ {
		fromField: "open",
		toField: "open"
	  }, {
		fromField: "close",
		toField: "close"
	  }, {
		fromField: "high",
		toField: "high"
	  }, {
		fromField: "low",
		toField: "low"
	  }, {
		fromField: "volume",
		toField: "volume"
	  }, {
		fromField: "value",
		toField: "value"
	  } ];
	  dataSet.color = "#d9d9d9";
	  dataSet.dataProvider = chartData;
	  dataSet.categoryField = "date";
	  /*dataSet.dataDateFormat = "MM-DD-YYYY JJ:NN:SS";*/
	  dataSet.borderAlpha = "1";

	  chart.dataSets = [ dataSet ];

	  // PANELS ///////////////////////////////////////////                                                  
	  stockPanel = new AmCharts.StockPanel();
	  stockPanel.title = "Value";

	  // graph of first stock panel
	  var graph = new AmCharts.StockGraph();
	  graph.type = "line";
	  graph.openField = "open";
	  graph.closeField = "close";
	  graph.highField = "high";
	  graph.lowField = "low";
	  graph.valueField = "close";
	  graph.lineColor = "#008fc5";
	  /*graph.fillColors = "#b2e7fa";*/
	  graph.fillColors = ["#b2e7fa","#fff"];
	  graph.negativeLineColor = "#f16e2d";
	  graph.negativeFillColors = "#f7b796";
	  graph.fillAlphas = 1;
	  graph.balloonText = "Open:<b>[[open]]</b><br>Close:<b>[[close]]</b><br>Low:<b>[[low]]</b><br>High:<b>[[high]]</b>";
	  graph.useDataSetColors = false;
	  stockPanel.addStockGraph( graph );
	  chart.panels = [ stockPanel ];

	  // OTHER SETTINGS ////////////////////////////////////
	  var sbsettings = new AmCharts.ChartScrollbarSettings();
	  sbsettings.graph = graph;
	  sbsettings.graphType = "line";
	  sbsettings.usePeriod = "WW";
	  chart.chartScrollbarSettings = sbsettings;

	  // Enable pan events
	  var panelsSettings = new AmCharts.PanelsSettings();
	  panelsSettings.panEventsEnabled = true;
	  chart.panelsSettings = panelsSettings;

	  // CURSOR
	  var cursorSettings = new AmCharts.ChartCursorSettings();
	  cursorSettings.valueBalloonsEnabled = true;
	  cursorSettings.valueLineBalloonEnabled = true;
	  cursorSettings.valueLineEnabled = true;
	  chart.chartCursorSettings = cursorSettings;

	  // PERIOD SELECTOR ///////////////////////////////////
	  var periodSelector = new AmCharts.PeriodSelector();
	  periodSelector.position = "bottom";
	  periodSelector.inputFieldsEnabled = false;
	  periodSelector.periods = [ {
		period: "DD",
		count: 7,
		label: "7d"
	  }, {
		period: "MM",
		count: 1,
		label: "1m"
	  }, {
		period: "MM",
		count: 3,
		label: "3m"
	  }, {
		period: "MM",
		count: 6,
		label: "6m"
	  }, {
		period: "YYYY",
		count: 1,
		label: "1y"
	  }, {
		period: "YYYY",
		count: 2,
		label: "2y"
	  }, {
		period: "YYYY",
		count: 3,
		label: "3y"
	  }, {
		period: "YTD",
		label: "YTD"
	  }, {
		period: "MAX",
		selected: true,
		label: "MAX"
	  } ];
	  chart.periodSelector = periodSelector;
	  
	  chart["export"] = {
		enabled: true
	  };
	  
	  chart.write( 'chartdiv' );
	}

	function addPanel() {
	  newPanel = new AmCharts.StockPanel();
	  newPanel.allowTurningOff = false;
	  newPanel.title = "Volume";
	  newPanel.showCategoryAxis = false;
	  newPanel.valueAxes.dashLength = 5;
		
	  var graph = new AmCharts.StockGraph();
	  graph.valueField = "volume";
	  graph.type = "column";
	  graph.fillAlphas = 1;
	  newPanel.addStockGraph( graph );

	  var legend = new AmCharts.StockLegend();
	  legend.markerType = "none";
	  legend.markerSize = 0;
	  newPanel.stockLegend = legend;

	  chart.addPanelAt( newPanel, 1 );
	  chart.validateNow();
	  /*document.getElementById( "addPanelButton" ).disabled = true;
	  document.getElementById( "removePanelButton" ).disabled = false;*/
	}

	function removePanel() {
	  chart.removePanel( newPanel );
	  chart.validateNow();

	  document.getElementById( "AddRemoveVolume" ).checked = false;
	  /*document.getElementById( "addPanelButton" ).disabled = false;
	  document.getElementById( "removePanelButton" ).disabled = true;*/
	}

	function changeType(type) {
	  chart.panels[0].stockGraphs[0].type = type;
	  chart.validateNow();
	}

$('#content_div').find('img').addClass("img-responsive");
$('#content_div fieldset').find('img').removeClass("img-responsive");

$(document).ready(function(){
	$("#email_form").validationEngine();
	reloadCaptcha();
	
	$('.rsave').click(function(){
		var aid = '116122000288';
		$.ajax({
			type : 'POST',
			url : '/article/save-user-article/',
			data : { aid:aid},
			success : function(data){
				if(data == 1){
				$('#savediv').hide();
				$('#savemsg').fadeIn().delay(3000).fadeOut();
				}else{
					$('#savediv').hide();
					$('#errormsg').show();
				}
			}
		});
	});
});

$('#email_popup').on('click', function(){
		$.ajax({
			type: 'POST',
			url: "/article/email",
			data:{ 
				'articleSeoStr' : $("#articleSeoStr").val(),
				'categorySeoStr' : $("#categorySeoStr").val(), 
				'name' : $("#name").val(), 
				'email' : $("#mail").val(),
				'friendEmail' : $("#friendEmail").val(), 
				'msg' : $("#msg").val(),
				'rcmtno' : $("#rcmtno").val(),
				'chitos_user':$("#chitos_user").val()
			},
			
			success: function(res){ 
								// $('.result_popup').fadeOut(1000);
								$('.result_popup').html( res ).show();
								// setTimeout(function(){
									// $("#emailModal").hide();
								// }, 3000);
			}
		});
});

function shownewsgraph_maindata(tabid){
	$('#mkt_tab_content_'+tabid).parents('.inner').find('.mkt_tab_content').hide();
	$('#showmkt_maintab_'+tabid).parents('.inner').find('.news_chart a').removeClass('active');
	$('#showmkt_maintab_'+tabid).addClass('active');
	$('#mkt_tab_content_'+tabid).fadeToggle();
}

function reloadCaptcha(){           
	$("#img_chitos").removeAttr("src");
	var randNo = Math.floor((Math.random() * 48) + 1);
	$("#img_chitos").attr("src", "/captcha/" + randNo);
	$("#rcmtno").val(randNo);
}

reloadCaptcha();

    function DropDown(el) {
        this.dd = el;
        this.initEvents();
    }
    DropDown.prototype = {
        initEvents: function () {
            var obj = this;

            obj.dd.on('click', function (event) {
                $(this).addClass('active');
                event.stopPropagation();
            });
        }
    }
    $(function () {
        var dd = new DropDown($('#dd'));
        $('.wrapper-dropdown-5').mouseleave(function () {
            // all dropdowns
            $('.wrapper-dropdown-5').removeClass('active');
        });
    });

    function mycarousel_initCallback(carousel) {
        carousel.clip.hover(function () {
            carousel.stopAuto();
        }, function () {
            carousel.startAuto();
        });
    }
    ;
    jQuery(document).ready(function () {
        $(".iifl_acc > h4 > a").click(function () {
            var iifl_acc_div = $(this).parent().parent().children('.iifl_acc_div');
            if (iifl_acc_div.is(":visible")) {
                $('.iifl_acc_div').slideUp();
            } else {
                $('.iifl_acc_div').slideUp();
                iifl_acc_div.slideDown();
            }
        });
        setTimeout("$('.wrapper-dropdown-5').addClass('active'),1000;", 200);
        setTimeout("$('.wrapper-dropdown-5').removeClass('active');", 1400);
        setTimeout("$('.wrapper-dropdown-5 .dropdown').css({'transition' : 'all 0.2s ease-out'});", 300);
        setTimeout("$('.wrapper-dropdown-5 .dropdown').css({'transition' : 'all 0.3s ease-out'});", 1500);

    });

    $("html").addClass("js");
    function Company_Tab(tabid) {
        $('#Company_Tab_Cont_' + tabid).parents('.inner').find('.Company_Tab_Cont').hide();
        $('#Company_Tab_' + tabid).parents('.inner').find('.com_tab_a a').removeClass('active');
        $('#Company_Tab_' + tabid).addClass('active');
        $('#Company_Tab_Cont_' + tabid).fadeToggle();
    }

    function showmkt_data(tabid) {
        $('#mkt_tabs_cont_' + tabid).parents('.mkt_tab_content').find('.mkt_tabs_cont').hide();
        $('#showmkt_tab_' + tabid).parents('.mkt_tab_content').find('.sub_tabs a').removeClass('active');
        $('#showmkt_tab_' + tabid).addClass('active');
        $('#mkt_tabs_cont_' + tabid).fadeToggle();
    }

    function showmkt_maindata(tabid) {
        $('#mkt_tab_content_' + tabid).parents('.inner').find('.mkt_tab_content').hide();
        $('#showmkt_maintab_' + tabid).parents('.inner').find('.mkt_main_tab a').removeClass('active');
        $('#showmkt_maintab_' + tabid).addClass('active');
        $('#mkt_tab_content_' + tabid).fadeToggle();
        var value = $('#showmkt_maintab_' + tabid).html();
    }

    function showmkt_maindata_tab(tabid) {
        $('#mkt_tab_content_tab_' + tabid).parents('.inner').find('.mkt_tab_content_tab').hide();
        $('#showmkt_maintab_tab_' + tabid).parents('.inner').find('.mkt_main_tab_tab a').removeClass('active');
        $('#showmkt_maintab_tab_' + tabid).addClass('active');
        $('#mkt_tab_content_tab_' + tabid).fadeToggle();
        var value = $('#showmkt_maintab_tab_' + tabid).html();
    }

    function showmkt_maindataCommodity(tabid) {
        $('#mkt_tab_content_' + tabid).parents('.inner').find('.mkt_tab_content').hide();
        $('#showmkt_maintab_' + tabid).parents('.inner').find('.mkt_main_tab a').removeClass('active');
        $('#showmkt_maintab_' + tabid).addClass('active');
        $('#mkt_tab_content_' + tabid).fadeToggle();
        var value = $('#showmkt_maintab_' + tabid).html();

    }

    function one_liner_msg(selectValue, selectId) {
        if (selectValue == 999999) {
            $('#' + selectId + '_LinkLbl').html('* Please Select ' + selectId + '.');
        } else {
            $('#' + selectId + '_LinkLbl').html('');
        }
    }
